<review>We stopped by this establishment at 6:30 pm one very rainy sunday.

Pull up to the curb, park, get out, and immediately someone pulls back the quaint beaded curtain and steps aside to let us in.  At first glance, the ...low-rent atmosphere may make others uneasy.  but Lo and behold, we found the ONE place with what we were looking for in stock. (Went to five other establishments that evening,and everyone else either did not have what we were looking for in stock, or did not stock it anymore (because people aren't "buying the heavy stuff anymore, because it is more material, hence more expensive") ...

These people not only had what we set out to acquire, but they had it at a fair market price, we ended up settling on a quality product at a great price.

The clerk, "Webster" was a great guy and very patient, working with great suggestions that matched our needs.   Excellent, polite customer service.

All around, it was a pleasant experience, and if the need arose, I would visit this establishment again.<//review>< response>

<Text>We have had a great experience at this studio. The instructors are all knowledgeable, kind and have appropriate expectations of our children. Both our kids thoroughly enjoy their classes and instructors, and look forward to each session. Dan Lockhart is especially great with the kids. He knows them, understands them, and speaks with them in a way they understand. I have seen many instructors or coaches in other activities who won't let children attempt something or continue to work toward something because they think they can't do it. Master Lockhart has high expectations of these kids and encourages them to push themselves; as a result my children have gained confidence, resilience and grit. I also truly appreciate the candor of the instructors; if a child does not try or does not do something well, they don't try to make it sound pretty - they will identify if it's not good - but on the other hand, if a child succeeds, tries hard, or is doing well, they will absolutely make it known. In a culture where my children get trophies just for showing up, it is a rare find to have someone identify the not-so-good and celebrate the true victories.</Text>< pictures>

< review>
Lockhart's Academy was recommended to me by my brother that took his son (now grown) here years before.  BEST recommendation ever.
I think anyone considering karate lessons for their children should come, bring them and watch a class or two.  Also, talk to other parents.  Some of us have been bringing our kids/grandkids here for years and can give you the honest story on the process, the instructors, the methods and the successes we've witnessed with our and everyone else's kids.
*My grandson has been attending karate lessons here for several years and is almost 13.  He is working his way up through the ranks and truly is enjoying the process and loves going.  It is not a cakewalk as there is a lot to master to progress.  That said, Master and Miss Lockhart and their staff are highly skilled, patient and dedicated to the journey for each individual student.
In addition to technical karate forms, general fitness and fun, the academy and their instructors wrap respect, focus, courage, honesty and responsibility for one's actions into every lesson.  All of this is done in a way that brings every type and personality of child into the fold and encourages/supports them to be their best and not give up.
In addition to karate skills, the personal growth in these kids is something to see.
So, only bring your kids here if you want to watch them learn solid karate skills and to be proud of themselves the real way-as they learn and earn it.
10 stars!!!<//review>

<Review>I greatly appreciate Master Lockhart and his diligence to the art. There are a myriad of martial art studios around, but I personally believe a studio should be chosen by the quality and the ethics of the instructor.

Master Lockhart is a man who has a gift of working with children. I am 30 years old and I attend the adult class and over 50% of the adults in my class have joined the studio after seeing the growth in their children, mentally and physically. I have two children ages four and six. My four year has attended the studio for over a year and the growth in my son is astounding.  My six year old has attended the studio for just over six months and she loves practicing her forms and working on counting to ten in Korean. As a parent we can only teach our kids so much, but I must say it is powerful to see Master Lockhart come along side your child to help them achieve goals as well as set goals.

As an adult I find his teaching extremely valuable, the principles taught in his studio have helped me in my personal life, work life and home life. I am a results-driven person, so I greatly appreciate hard work. Lockhart‚Äôs academy is a studio where you earn each rank given. Master Lockhart does not show favoritism. Each person that walks through the door of his studio is respected and treated as an equal and this is the attitude of the staff as well.

Master Lockhart is an abundantly humble leader who cares about the success of the students and their families. This man is a true leader and the leadership shows by the attitude in his staff and the humility of his students. I greatly appreciate the way he trains students into becoming teachers no matter the age. One of my first days in the class there was a young man about 10 years old, who  was tasked to walk us through a couple of techniques. I was so pleased by the great level detail in this young man. I feel blessed to know that a portion of the next generation of teens and young adults that are a part of Lockhart‚Äôs academy will be respectful and carry an attitude of humility.

‚ÄúA leader is one who knows the way, goes the way, and shows the way‚Äù.

Thank you Master Lockhart for your diligence and respect for the art.

Respectfully,
The Perry Family<//Review>< rating>

<Time>1433759039532</Time><rate>4</rate><text>Crepes Sans Frontieres is tucked away in the Spring Arcade Building (closer to Broadway than Spring). The building is undergoing renovations so don't mind the construction across the hall.

The Service was slow, but I suppose that was to be expected during the lunch hour. The nice part is that my group and I were seated right away without having to wait for a table to open.

The shop itself is on the smaller end and has small tables. I was with a group of 4 people and we managed to fit 4 plates and 3 glasses of water on it. I don't think we could have squeezed a fourth glass in though.

I ordered the L'Anglaise crepe (bacon, eggs and Monterrey jack cheese) and ginger-lemonade. The crepe was delicious and filled with bacon! It is served with a small salad that I felt lacked some dressing.

The ginger-lemonade tasted a bit bitter and had a kick to it from the ginger. I don't think I'll be ordering it again, but it is worth a try if you are into bitter drinks.<//text><Pictures>None< /Pictures><response>None<//response>< Gmap_id>

< Name>
Remi Tran< /Name>
<Date>1513551464957</Date><Rating>1</Rating>< Review>
Stumbled onto Spring Arcade while in downtown LA this week to see a chiropractor, and was pleasantly surprised to see a few nice little restaurants in this quaint little arcade.

I was alone and was looking for a simple lunch, settled on Crepes San Frontieres when I saw that they had some good vegetarian options.
I ordered the mushroom panini which I felt was a mistake, should have gone with the server's suggestion of the crepe instead. The bread was a little too hard for my liking. I asked for a cup of hot water with a slice of lemon and was glad that they gave me a large cup. However, they failed to tell me that there was a charge of $1.00 per cup of hot water and when I asked for a refill, they charged me again for the refill!!
Pretty absurd don't you think?!!

I wouldn't have minded being charged $1.00 for the hot water but it would have been nice if they had told me about it first, but the second charge for a top up which wasn't even a full cup is just ridiculous! It's not the money at this point, but I hate being 'nickeled and dime-ed'!!

I didn't review the line items on my check when I got it until the next day! I was appalled! While I understand that it is a business and they have to make money, but to nickel and dime your customers is a very bad business approach!! Especially in this day and age with the likes of Yelp and google reviews!

I will never step into your restaurant again and will never recommend anyone. In fact, I will always remember my experience and pass it along to anyone who mentions the name of your restaurant.<//Review>
